utilities used
pygame 2.1.0 (SDL 2.0.16, Python 3.9.5)
Hello from the pygame community. https://www.pygame.org/contribute.html
Welcome to Hasami Shogi, a project by Eli Mills.
To get started, select a game mode.

Please select from the following options:
[1] Visual Mode: Player vs Player.
[2] Visual Mode: Player vs AI.
[3] Visual Mode: AI vs AI.
[4] Terminal Mode: Player vs Player.
Enter 'exit' to exit.
